Huang Bangjun Passes Away 154

Huang Bangjun, a young sociologist from Xingguo, Jiangxi Province, was from a poor family but loved to study and wrote extensively. He studied at Guanghua University and Jinan University in Shanghai and was highly regarded by his teachers and friends. He translated "Introduction to Sociology" and "The Experience of Beauty" and wrote "Mother" and "A Materialistic Observation of Women's Lives," etc. Philosopher Li Shicen, sociologist Wu Zelin, political scientist Wang Zaoshi, and historian Yao Mingda all cherished him and hoped he would achieve great things. Unexpectedly, due to overwork, he suddenly contracted severe typhoid fever and was hospitalized at Renji Hospital. After being ill for several days, he passed away at noon yesterday. His sister, Ms. Huang Xinmian, and her husband personally visited and mourned him, weeping loudly. They plan to have his posthumous works published by the Women's Bookstore and are seeking elegies and condolences from friends to be printed in a book of mourning. A memorial service will be held in the near future. Donations and elegies can be sent to the Women's Bookstore at 29 Yuanmingyuan Road, Shanghai.

Inspection Report of the China Land Reclamation Bank 155

The issuance department and the business department of the China Land Reclamation Bank have always been completely separated. According to the articles of association, the cash reserve should be above 70% and the guarantee reserve below 30%. On the 10th of this month, accountant Wang Zikang, together with the representatives of the board of directors and supervisors Xu Ji, and Xu Busun, conducted an inspection with the following results: the total amount of exchange coupons issued was 4,795,000 silver dollars, and the total amount of exchange coupon reserves was 4,795,000 silver dollars, including 3,821,388 silver dollars in cash reserves and 973,612 silver dollars in guarantee reserves. The cash reserve accounts for slightly more than 79% of the total, and the guarantee reserve accounts for slightly less than 21%.

Hong Shihhao Authors English-Language Chinese Commercial Law 169

Lawyer Hong Shihhao has recently authored a book titled "Chinese Commercial Law" in English, totaling over 300 pages. It is divided into ten chapters, totaling fifty-eight sections. The content includes the history of commercial law, contracts, deposits, sales, partnerships, companies, bills, commercial crimes, trademarks, insurance, banking, and maritime law. The appendix includes a table of current laws and regulations, listing the dates of promulgation and implementation. All current commercial laws and regulations are listed in detail. The entire book uses current legal provisions as the warp and the interpretations of the former Daliyuan and the Supreme Court as the weft, and each section is accompanied by clear examples. It is compiled in a thesis style, following the classification methods of English and American law. Famous figures in Chinese and foreign legal circles, such as Cai Yuanpei, British Chief Justice Lord Granton, and Chief Superintendent of the Public Works Department John S., have all written prefaces, praising it as an unprecedented work on current Chinese law in English. It has now been published, and many domestic and foreign lawyers have already purchased a copy each. Sales are strong. Major bookstores in this city are all selling it on consignment.

Letter Received

To the Editor:

Having read your newspaper's local news column of September 6, which published a "Truth about the Housing Dispute in Xincheng Lane", the matter is completely contrary to the truth. It was found that Gu Pingzhang is one of the defendants and has no right to blame this lawyer. The phrase "Article 2, Clause 2 of the Mediation Law" was mistakenly written as "Article 2, Clause 3" by the clerk drafting the pleading, which can be corrected by application. Subsequently, the court ordered an investigation by the Social Bureau into the facts of the mediation. This is the truth of the case. But the news reported that the mediation was rejected, but it is not known on what basis. As the matter concerns reputation, please publish a letter of correction.

Lawyers Xia Zhezhen and Huang Sicheng, September 9.

Page 21

Free Talk: How Should We Save the Country? 丨Free Talk Special Issue丨

Opening Remarks 173

—Juan

More than ten years ago, shocked by the May 9th Twenty-One Demands, I wrote a volume of "Diary of a Stateless Slave" (published by Zhonghua Book Company), in which I acted as a Korean-style stateless slave and tearfully described the tragic state of China after being destroyed by Japan. At the time, I said in the conclusion, "May this ideal forever remain an ideal." Who knew that on the night of September 18th last year, Japan suddenly invaded the Eastern Provinces, resulting in a year of various horrors and tragedies. My ideal from more than ten years ago seems to be gradually becoming a reality!

But although I have played the role of an ideal stateless slave, I do not want to be a real stateless slave. So I drew my sword and struck the ground, scratched my head and asked the sky, wandering around the room day and night, painfully thinking, "How should we save the country?" Unfortunately, I have the will to save the country, but lack the ability to reverse fate. After thinking hard for three days and three nights, I still couldn't come up with an effective plan. There was nothing I could do but borrow the pages of Free Talk to publicly solicit ideas. Within ten days, I received more than three hundred letters. Now, I will select some of the practical ones and disclose them. I hope everyone will act quickly and catch up, and work hard together on this great work of saving the country.

How Should We Save the Country? 174

— Mingsan

丨Better to Rely on Yourself Than on Others丨

The only thing in the world you can truly rely on is yourself. Seeking pity from others, seeking help from others, only leads to digging your own grave!

"Not afraid of a thousand arrows, only afraid of one heart," we should unite automatically, encourage each other, and discipline each other. We must know that "the backbone of the country is the warehouse of the collective power of the citizens."

Don't think that because you are "insignificant," you cannot save the country. Know that a diligent worker may be stronger than an important person who sleeps on a steel-spring bed and shouts for resistance.

We must "look far ahead and stand firm on the ground," identify a path, and walk forward with big steps. One day, there will be "an eye for an eye, and blood for blood" day!

The only object of saving the country right now is to increase wealth and intelligence. Student strikes and worker strikes reduce the source of national intelligence and the source of national productivity, both of which are unacceptable!

We must vow to never buy or sell enemy goods, and not to engage in any professional cooperation with enemies. Before we die, don't forget to leave a will to our descendants!

We should actively exercise our bodies. In peacetime, the body is a tool for work, and in wartime, it is a weapon for killing enemies. Sympathy and assistance are not empty words on paper and in mouths. We should practically help the "blood and ironless" volunteers in our Eastern Provinces!

My Suggestions for Saving the Country 175

— Qiantaisheng

丨Still Depends on the People丨

I have beaten a big gong and asked all the people, saying, "How should we save the country?" Their answers are all: shaking their heads, sighing, and saying, "There is no way!"

The so-called "sighing" of the people is just their way of expressing a passive approach. If we really want to save the country, isn't the greatest strength still in the people?

(1) Use Domestic Goods: Gandhi's naked body wearing Indian homespun is one such method. We don't have to wear British leather shoes, we have homemade cloth shoes; we don't have to eat "Beauty" brand ice cream, we can boil a cup of plain water; we don't have to wear imported yarns, we have Chinese homespun or silk. To go back 36,000 miles, cutting the electric light wire and lighting a vegetable oil lamp is not a shameful thing!

(2) National Salvation Fund: Donated voluntarily by the people to alleviate the country's current deficiencies. The funds are still kept by the people themselves, and their use is jointly managed by the people and the government, such as expanding military equipment, opening factories, reclaiming wasteland, and promoting industry.

(3) Compulsory Education: Investigate the school-age children across the country and send them to school compulsorily; for adults who have not received education, people's night schools should be promoted. The school's funding and preparations should be voluntarily created and supervised by the people!

(4) Conscription System: All people in the country should receive military training for a considerable number of years so that all people have military common sense; minors should also be forced to receive physical education. Make the whole country strong reserves, with only a small number of formal troops.

Two "Self" Methods for Saving the Country 176

— Jiang Jieru

丨"Self" "From This Moment On"丨

To save China, we must first make China's economic organization sound and stable! In other words: on the one hand, we must produce as much as possible, and on the other hand, we must strive to save money. This is the strategy for saving China; it should also be a common goal recognized by those engaged in saving the country's work. To accomplish this goal, it is necessary for the entire nation to work together. However, the so-called "national strength" is a collection of individual strengths. The first problem of the Chinese people is: everyone is responsible for saving the country, but forgets themselves! Everyone does not do their best, and the strength of the nation cannot be born; the country cannot be saved!

Secondly, to accomplish this goal, it is necessary to have a long-term effort. However, "traveling far begins with the near." Ten or twenty years are linked together from one second and one minute. The second problem of the Chinese people is: recalling the past and hoping for the future, but neglecting the present. Following the old ways and sitting idle, the national situation will become increasingly dangerous and unsavable!

Therefore, if the work of saving the country is to have practical effects in the future, the Chinese people must abandon the two major problems mentioned above. Under the commonly recognized goals mentioned earlier, every person's "self" must "from this moment on" work hard!

Basic Work for National Salvation 177

— Yang Yusheng

丨Respectfully Propose Four Creeds丨

To still speak of national salvation today, the call for national salvation comes only from the mouths of a very few intellectuals, and yet we expect them to have practical solutions; putting pen to paper on this matter fills me with endless sorrow. This is not to sing high-sounding tunes or deliberately make alarming statements; it is because in China's current situation, those in positions of power are themselves unable to unite and disdain leading the masses; the masses, lacking strong organization, are at a loss as to how to save themselves, resulting in a state of fragmentation. Therefore, the most important task for national salvation today is to awaken the masses, rectify their ranks, strengthen their organization, each fulfilling their duties, each exerting their strength, striving to eliminate selfish desires and such bad habits as frivolity, obstinacy, and laziness, and only then can something be achieved. Here, I tentatively propose four creeds for basic national salvation work that everyone can do, to seek the wisdom of enlightened individuals and ask for their opinion on the matter:

Students, quickly read more books;

Merchants, above all, value integrity;

Farmers and workers, each do their best;

The entire nation must abstain from extravagance.

We, disregarding all adverse circumstances, not expecting guidance or assistance from the government, not aiming high or grand, but standing tall and each striving in basic work. The four creeds mentioned above are all easy to accomplish, and everyone can do them and easily achieve practical results. If even this is not desired or deemed worthy of doing, then everything else is empty talk and fantasy, and please do not speak of national salvation again!

National Salvation Methods That Everyone Can Do 178

— Shuang Hong

丨National Salvation Begins with the People Saving Themselves丨

Wake up! National salvation, national salvation, now is no longer the time to engage in empty theoretical talk! To save the nation, we must first start with the people saving themselves!

(1) Young students! Quickly strive to study diligently! Laboriously research academics! Stop staging the farce of expelling and beating up principals!

(2) Sacred workers! Concentrate on your work! Increasing your own production is increasing the nation's production! Unfortunate labor disputes, do not let them happen again!

(3) Industrialists and general merchants! Straighten your consciences, stop smuggling inferior goods to pass off as domestic goods!

(4) Modern girls! Stop spending your precious time on applying lipstick and mixing cosmetics! Put more effort into beneficial work! Those studying should concentrate on their studies, those managing household affairs should concentrate on household affairs, those with jobs should concentrate on their jobs.

(5) All other people! You do not really need to sleep on firewood and taste gall. In this era of national and social economic decline, let us all "save the nation through thrift"! If everyone can live thriftily with simple clothes and coarse food, it is guaranteed to be more effective than shouting "sleeping on firewood and tasting gall."

The above matters are things that everyone can do, and if everyone is determined to save themselves, then the "nation" will be "saved" without needing to be saved!

My Principles for National Salvation 179

— Zhang Qian

丨A Total of Four丨

First, in everything, do not hold onto selfish and self-serving ideas. The concept of "selfishness and self-interest" is truly extremely prevalent in society. All corruption, fraud, perversion of justice, and dereliction of duty arise from the word "self." How can such people save the nation? National salvation must first mean "no self"!

Second, live a simple, plain, diligent, and hardworking life. Current living standards are truly making people more and more delicate. Food must be good to be palatable, houses must be good to be willing to live in. Good must be better, and scrutiny must be deeper. I ask, is this situation in line with China's current state? Can such people talk about national salvation? They are the same as selfish and self-serving people, and if they get a position, they will only desperately enrich themselves.

Third, do not use foreign goods. For all daily necessities, not only should we absolutely not buy enemy goods, but we should also try our best not to buy any foreign goods. When we love domestic goods, we can cultivate some vitality for national capital and suffer one less layer of exploitation by imperialists.

Fourth, strive to promote science. China suffers in everything because its fundamental material civilization is backward, especially in science and industry. Although new industries are gradually rising domestically now, in China, where there is no scientific foundation, it is like building a tower on sand, not very reliable. We, the educated, must each do our best in society to promote the awareness that the outside world is a world of science, that science should be loved, and that science should be respected, fathers exhorting their sons, elder brothers telling their younger brothers. If this kind of force is widely planted among the people, there will be countless engineers in the future, creating a solid industrial base.

Patriotic Novel

The Black Flag Army 180

— Qin Shouou

After the calamity, on the streets of S-port, colorful red lanterns, shops playing the tune of "Meng Jiangnü Seeking Her Husband" to attract customers, radio singing, everything was gone. Day and night, swaggering through the streets were either red-eyed, mad-looking J-nation army and navy, or J-nation ronin wearing tattered suits, so proud that they didn't know there were other nations in the world. They—from children to old women—had already seen the entire S-port as a soybean-sized grain! Moon-shaped flags were waving everywhere.

The retreat of the 32nd Army allowed the J-nation army to occupy S-port without any effort; hundreds of thousands of citizens immediately fell into the irrecoverable realm of being slaves of a conquered nation. The corpses of naked women were piled high in a large temple on Wuri Road. Gunshots rang out on the streets at any time. The life of every Chinese person was as worthless as a pebble.

This night, dark clouds shrouded the sky over S-port, and heavy rain poured down as if it were being dumped. The J-nation aircraft that had been flaunting their power in the blue sky all day had hidden without a trace; the J-nation sentries standing on the streets all hid behind telephone poles, trembling.

Suddenly, the sound of engines whirred, dozens of white lights flashed in mid-air, and hundreds of pounds of bombs flew down continuously.

"Boom:: Boom::" The J-nation army's airport was destroyed, the headquarters was bombed, and the tank depot also caught fire! Countless J-nation army and navy soldiers, abandoning their armor and helmets, fled desperately in the heavy rain, pushing and shoving, yelling. The so-called might of the Imperial Army was swept away!

Then, from the northwest, a cannon fire that sounded distinctly different from ordinary artillery roared like a string of pearls! Main streets were filled with skirmishes between plainclothes team J-nation army and ronin. Hand grenades, machine guns, and mortars sounded denser and denser, and the fire stretched for seven or eight miles. The rain turned into oil, not only failing to extinguish the fire but increasing the flames.

Before dawn, the J-nation army on the northwestern front completely collapsed. Suddenly appearing, deep black, strange aircraft dropped heavy bombs on their heads in rows, destroying and burying them in teams. The tortures they had inflicted on the Chinese army a few days ago were now befalling them!

Outside Mazongkou, in the Qipu River, hundreds of steel-made small steamers also charged in, firing extremely fierce artillery fire, divided into several teams, and attacking the J-nation warships anchored there; flexible steel cables flew out from the small boats, hooking onto the sides of the warships, and many warriors carrying machine guns that were firing climbed onto the warships from the steel cables, and extremely powerful hand grenades were thrown from their hands.

This strange tactic immediately conquered warships weighing several thousand tons, and the navy was resolved! By afternoon, every J-nation person with a gun had become an unarmed prisoner. Hundreds of purely black fighter planes, after clearing out the enemy's air force, arranged themselves in four large characters in the sky, "Long Live China."

Chinese heroes wearing black military uniforms and holding black flags had driven out the enemy and taken back the entire S-port!

This was the great victory of the Black Flag Army, which had been trained for fifteen years and had never participated in a civil war.

Yesterday, the U.S. cotton market was strong and active. It was strong initially due to good news from Liverpool, then softened due to selling by Japanese merchants. Futures rose by 16 to 19 points, and spot prices rose by 15 points. English cotton futures fell by 26-27 points, and spot prices fell by 72 points. Egyptian cotton spot prices fell by 70 points. Indian cotton initially fell due to speculative and brokerage selling, but then recovered due to buying by Japanese merchants. Bengals fell by 26 rupees, Oomras fell by 30.5 rupees, and Broach fell by 34 rupees. Recorded by telegraph (9th).

U.S. Government Cotton Estimate for Last Week 500,000 Bales Higher Than Forecast 190

Market Price Plunges 105 Points

New York, September 9th telegram reports on the cotton market situation for the week: Reports of storms in Texas during the holiday, the strength of the Liverpool market, and forecasts of reduced cotton production caused raw cotton prices to rise. However, since yesterday's government report was released, large-scale liquidations have followed. According to this report, the expected new cotton harvest is slightly higher than previously anticipated. This is seen as a report that lowers market prices. As prices fell, traders bought in, and those who were short also actively covered their positions, but demand was not strong. Some believe that the cotton production estimate is 500,000 bales higher than forecast, and this estimate clearly has room for revision. In the future, after the revision, the cotton market will once again be dominated by optimism about the prospects for general trade. However, some also believe that buyers will be more cautious because they anticipate that hedging sales will increase when new cotton comes on the market more vigorously. At the same time, continuous reports of reduced cotton quality indicate that cotton crops have been developing poorly since September 1st. If the weather does not improve, the official report released in October will show even lower production figures. The weekend statistics are listed below (in thousands of bales):

Grain and Rice Market: Strong Sales Turn Weak 191

Shanghai South: Yesterday, there were still many boats arriving from various routes. Sales in this street were sluggish because the new *yangjian* rice was weak, and the old and broken *gong* rice also showed signs of weakness. The arrival of new *geng* rice was not large, and transactions became more active when the market opened. The arrival and sales of *xinhetan* rice were even. There were few shipments of early and late rice. Due to the sharp declines in recent days, top-quality rice saw some movement, and prices remained the same as before. New Gate: Yesterday, twenty-three or four boats arrived in *Xiang*. Most of them came from Jiangyin, Kunshan, Jiashan, and other areas. Urban and rural stores are selling because the Mid-Autumn Festival is approaching. It is the time for companies to settle accounts. The stockpiles of *Changxi Beigeng* and *Sutong* rice are still abundant, and people's sentiment is calm. The prices of new *geng*, new *du*, and *yangjian* rice have fallen by one or two *jiao*. There is not much stock of *tanbu jian* rice, and the price is slightly less than a *jiao*. However, the price of *bianyuan* rice has moved slightly, and the price has risen slightly more than a *jiao*.

Foreign Rice Becoming Gradually More Popular 192

Both North and South ports are handling shipments ::: This street is stagnant.

Yesterday, the foreign rice market was in a stagnant situation. Because both the North and South groups were inquiring, although the quantity was not large, the market had become active, and people's sentiment was optimistic. However, there was still a lot of stock in the market, and the arrival of *hexiadu jian* rice caused the market price to fall. The price of foreign rice was dragged down by it. Yesterday, the sales on this street were stagnant. However, after the guest groups saw the Shanghai price recover slightly, it was feasible to handle transportation. The total daily transaction volume was 2,000 bags of small *jiaomi* rice, 1,000 bags of No. 1 Saigon rice, 300 bags of Siamese rice, and 80 bags of *Xiangmi* rice. Local businesses on this street only handle a small amount of small *jiaomi* rice. The rest is handled by the three major groups from the northern port of Yantai and the southern ports of Shantou and Xiamen. The price is firm.

Wheat Flour Futures Trading Turns Active 193

Shandong group buys spot flour.

Yesterday, after the flour market opened in the morning, the prices for various months stabilized. Because the prices of foreign wheat fluctuated by about one *jiao*, and because the gold price rebounded in recent days, the exchange rate narrowed. The major factories generally stood aside and did not offer prices, which stabilized people's sentiment and made trading slightly more active. The prices for various months were about five *li* higher than the previous day. When the market opened in the afternoon, people's sentiment became even more active because the Shandong group bought spot flour (Fuxin had no surplus and required prior registration). It was also rumored that Yutong's machine donations were suspended, and the U.S. government estimated a decrease in the wheat harvest. Due to these various reasons, the market atmosphere was stimulated. However, because rice prices are falling daily and flour is a supplementary food for the people, there is no hope of excessive price increases. As a result, the price for this month rose by 1.25 *fen*, October and November rose by 1.75 *fen*, December rose by 2 *fen*, January rose by 1.5 *fen*, and February rose by 1.75 *fen*.

Wheat Market Lacks Orders and Difficult to Develop 194

Yesterday, the wheat futures market was generally stable. Because the prices of foreign wheat did not fluctuate much, trading in various months was unusually quiet. Only this month was considered lively, while the rest only had one price because the wheat market seemed to lack orders. Without real goods, it is difficult for trading to develop. As a result, the price for this month was 1 *fen* higher than the previous day, October remained unchanged, November was slightly lower by 1 *fen*, December remained unchanged, January was higher by 1 *fen*, and February remained unchanged. The spot wheat market saw two periods of silence, with no trading taking place.

Sugar Market: Refined Ice Sugar Already Arrived 196

Yesterday, the sugar market was stabilizing because the standard levy was stable and the Dutch exchange rate was rising. The guild’s set price for ordinary grade #24 coarse granulated white sugar was Tls. 14.45, while the purchasing price for the in-port was only Tls. 14.44, again resulting in a stalemate. The Exchange posted a price of Tls. 13.3 for over 60 packages of Huizhou white sugar from the Chaozhou group and Tls. 9.3 for dozens of crates of brick green sugar. Deliveries of refined ice sugar have been rare for some time. Upon investigation, Taikoo and NanNing’s imports had already received a batch of over 400 boxes, but because the landed costs are quite high, they have yet to convert.

Silk and Tea: Foreign Firms' Silk Sales Quiet 197

Yesterday, the silk market was quiet because there were no overseas telegrams, and European and American firms were watching. Only the Gong'an firm imported 20 bales of Tongjun brand 13-15 denier Shanghai white factory silk at Tls. 665 per bale. The Huzhou factory imported 10 bales of Jinma brand 13-18 denier Shanghai white factory silk at Tls. 620 per bale.

In the last few days, various Yangtze River liners have imported 730 bales of yellow and white coarse silk shipped from Hankou.

Pingshui Group's Sales Active to America 198

Yesterday, sales of Huzhou Pingshui green tea to American firms became active again. A major group, consisting of Jinlong Foreign Firm and China Tea Company, purchased over 5,000 cases. There were also scattered transactions in other varieties such as Pearl Tea and Needle Eyebrow. The market for green teas from the Lu Group and high-grade Mei teas from Tunxi and Sui'an was slightly more active, but sales of Wuyuan Guang goods remained stagnant.

Piece Goods: Woolen Fabrics Sales Surge 199

Yesterday, the market atmosphere at the Tongyi Guild for woolen fabrics was excellent. Transactions between buyers and sellers were frequent. Sales to local customers surged because the weather was cool and retail sales had started. Wholesale and retail business increased sharply, and all goods were active. Yesterday, substantial orders were placed for Walter Cloth, Serge, Raincoat Cloth, Melton, Overcoating, and Novelty Tweed, making the market very lively.

In addition, 200 cases of new woolen fabrics, including serge and tweed, arrived yesterday on the Sumori.

Metals: Lead Market Stable 200

Yesterday, the trading of metals was more active among the Changjiang gangs. The number of transactions was also higher. The northern groups of Tianjin, Yantai and Beiping were still buying less, although there were slight transactions by the Fujian groups, the amount was not large. Building trades in this street and odd-lot business also showed no improvement, so the market situation was quite scattered.

Overseas reports strengthen for lead. Recent telegrams from overseas indicate that lead is being offered at $47 per ton and that the market is very firm. It is reported that merchants from South Asia and India have purchased 500-600 tons, and domestic merchants here had previously purchased over 700 tons at around $44-45. Since they have not finalized those contracts, Shanghai standards are heard to be offered at Tls. 12.3. Therefore, the trend is still stable. After local Hunan lead rose with foreign lead, paint companies, yellow lead factories, and printing houses on this street have begun to purchase it. Therefore, the number of transactions has been strong in recent days, and the price is between Tls. 11.75 and 12 per picul.

British tinplate is set to ship 5,000 boxes. Trade in 90-pound British tinplate has been quite lively recently. The foreign price is in recent reports still very low, so merchants have placed orders to import 5,000 boxes at 14 shillings per box. Retail prices are at 14 shillings, 3-4 pence.

The offering price for new silver dollars is depressed. Since sales of new silver dollars have been sluggish in the North, shipments have been severely impacted. Business from southern merchants has not progressed much, and the market is quiet. The current market price is estimated at Tls. 4.75, and there are few buyers. However, it is found that merchants must import at around Tls. 5.5-5.6, so the price is almost a tael underwater.
